5) **Anticipated Changes**
- The exact property selection may evolve as listings are reviewed.
- Financing approach may shift depending on available equity or market conditions.
- Service providers (legal, moving, utilities) can be adjusted based on user preferences or cost constraints.
- Final budget may vary slightly depending on closing costs and additional fees.

**Property Transfer Tax (Ontario Land Transfer Tax):**  
- For a CAD 725,000 property, the estimated LTT is approximately **CAD 10,475**.

**Other Typical Costs:**
